<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะผะตะปัะบะฝััั.html>ะผะตะปัะบะฝัฬัั</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">melสนknรบtสน</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะผะตะปัะบะฐัั.html>ะผะตะปัะบะฐฬัั</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to flash, to gleam</li>
<li>to flit, to fly (past)</li>
<li>to loom, to turn up</li>
<li>to appear for a moment, to be glimpsed fleetingly</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะผะตะฝััะตะฒะธะบ.html>ะผะตะฝััะตะฒะธฬะบ</a> (11251)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ะผะตะฝััั.html>ะผะตะฝัฬัั</a> (1967)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mฤna</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะผะตะฝััั.html>ะผะตะฝัฬัั</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">menjรกtสน</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะฟะพะผะตะฝััั.html>ะฟะพะผะตะฝัฬัั</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะพะฑะผะตะฝััั.html>ะพะฑะผะตะฝัฬัั</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to swap, to barter (to give something to another person and take something in return)</li>
<li>to replace, to substitute or supersede (to get rid of an old thing or person and get a new one)</li>
<li>to modify, to change, to transform, to alter (to make something different gradually)</li>
<li>to exchange, to recapture (to lose one or more pieces or pawns almost simultaneously with the opponent)</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ะผะตัะตัะธ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mereti</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*merti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mer-</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ะผะตัะตัั.html>ะผะตัะตฬัั</a></strong> โข (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">merรฉtสน</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to die, to perish (in large numbers)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to stand still, to sink, to miss a beat</li></ol>
